Fire (archis), day time, the bright half of the month (sukla pakс╣гa), Uttar─Бyaс╣Зa and the year,
thence Vayu, Surya, Chandra and then Lightning,
Varuna, Indra, Praj─Бpati or Brahma –
having traversed this path in the order given above,
the self crosses the river Viraja;
then follows the wonder that defies (all description in words.)

English

Thus the Lord who lives in the heart
and who is full of love (for the J─лva )
starts -
with the self who desires mukti
and who has entered into the n─Бdi in the head
from out of Brahmapuri, namely, the gross body,
by the Brahma N─Бdi,
which is, as it were, the main gate (of that city).

In this He resembles a king
who walks to and fro
with his charming child in his arms.

Espa├▒ol

As├н, el Se├▒or que vive en el coraz├│n
y que est├б lleno de amor (para el J─лva)
comienza -
con el yo que desea mukti
y quien ha entrado en el n─Бdi en la cabeza
De fuera de Brahmapuri, a saber, el cuerpo bruto,
por el Brahma N─Бdi,
que es, por as├н decirlo, la puerta principal (de esa ciudad).

En esto se parece a un rey
quien camina de un lado a otro
con su encantador hijo en sus brazos.

рдЗрддрд┐

English

As has been said in the following verses :-

“The self passes through a beautiful opening
in the centre of the sphere of the sun.”

Espa├▒ol

Como se ha dicho en los siguientes vers├нculos:-

“El yo pasa por una hermosa apertura
en el centro de la esfera del sol “.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЗрддреНрдердВ рд╕рдорд╕реНрдд-рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдХ-рдирд┐рд╡реГрддреНрддрд┐-рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдХрдВ рд╕реНрд╡–рд╕реНрд╡-рд░реВрдкрд╛рд╡рд┐рд░реНрднрд╛рд╡-рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдХрдВ рдЪ

рд╕реНрд╡-рдордиреЛ-рд░рдерд╛рдиреБрд░реВрдкрдореН рдПрддрдиреН-рдордиреЛ-рд░рде-рдЧреЛрдЪрд░рдВ рдХреИрдЩреНрдХрд░реНрдпрдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рдВ
рдпрд╛рд╡рджреН-рдЖрддреНрдо-рднрд╛рд╡рд┐рддрдпрд╛ рд╜рдиреБрдЧреГрд╣реНрдп,

English

Then the Lord blesses him
with the grant of all such services
as were desired by him
and as are agreeable to Himself,
having previously removed all hindrances
and enabled him to attain his essential nature in a manifest form,
and without any limitations of place, time and circumstance,
so that these services may last as long as his soul lasts.

Espa├▒ol

Entonces el Se├▒or lo bendice
con la concesi├│n de todos estos servicios
como lo deseaban
y como son de acuerdo para s├н mismo,
habiendo eliminado previamente todos los obst├бculos
y le permiti├│ alcanzar su naturaleza esencial en una forma manifiesta,
y sin limitaciones de lugar, tiempo y circunstancia,
para que estos servicios puedan durar mientras su alma dure.

it is said also that

“those who attain mukti
give up the worship of the incarnational form (Vibhava),

and finally after the worship of the Vy┼лha,

renunciar a la adoraci├│n de la forma encarnacional (Vibhava),
proceda de all├н a la adoraci├│n del Vy┼лha

“рдЗрдордВ рдкреБрд░реБрд╖рд╛рд░реНрдердВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрд╕реНрдпрд╛рдордГ”

English

It becomes an end in itself,
as it produces a keen delight in knowing that, very soon,
the supreme goal begged for at the time of prapatti
will be attained.
In this respect it is like counting the days before the ensuing wedding.

Espa├▒ol

Se convierte en un fin en s├н mismo,
Como produce una gran delicia al saber que, muy pronto,
El objetivo supremo rog├│ en el momento de Prapatti ser├б alcanzado.
A este respecto, es como contar los d├нas previos a la boda que sigue.

English

Of this meditation on the path to mukti,
the state of S─лt─Б is an example (of whom it is said):

“It looked as if S─лt─Б was driving in the chariot of her mind
drawn by her desires which were like fleet horses,
towards ┼Ъr─лR─Бma, the greatest of kings,
who was aware of his nature
that always insisted on protecting those that sought his help”.

Espa├▒ol

De esta meditaci├│n en el camino a Mukti,
El estado de s─лt─Б es un ejemplo (de quien se dice):

“Parec├нa que S─лt─Б conduc├нa en el carro de su mente
dibujado por sus deseos que eran como caballos de flota,
Hacia ┼Ъr─лr─Бma, el m├бs grande de los reyes,
Qui├йn era consciente de su naturaleza
Eso siempre insisti├│ en proteger a aquellos que buscaban su ayuda “.

+++(рд╕реНрд╡рд░реНрдЧ-рдЧрд╛рдорд┐-)+++рдкрд┐рддреГ-рдкрде-+++(рдХреВрдк-)+++рдШрдЯреА-рдпрдиреНрддреНрд░рд╛рд░реЛрд╣рд╛рд╡рд░реЛрд╣-рдкрд░рд┐рднреНрд░рдореИрдГ
рдирд┐рд░рдп-рдкрджрд╡реА-рдпрд╛рддрд╛рдпрд╛рдд-рдХреНрд░рдореИрд╢реН рдЪ рдирд┐рд░рдиреНрддрд░реИрдГ ред

English

We become exhausted by frequent ascent (to svarga) and descent back to the earth
along the path of the Pitс╣Ыs (the path of smoke)
like the water-pot going up and down the well by the rotation of the water-wheel.
(We become exhausted likewise) by incessant journey, to and fro, along the route to hell.
(So) Hari makes the various deities (on the shining path of archis) entertain us who are so exhausted
and at length confers bliss on us
by keeping us, as it were, under His shade
which is like the shade of a sandal tree.

Espa├▒ol

Nos agotamos por el ascenso frecuente (a Svarga) y el descenso de regreso a la tierra
a lo largo del camino de los Pitс╣Ыs (el camino del humo)
Al igual que el bote de agua subiendo y bajando por la rotaci├│n de la rueda de agua.
(Nos agotamos tambi├йn) por un viaje incesante, de aqu├н para all├б, a lo largo de la ruta al infierno.
(Entonces) Hari hace que las diversas deidades (en el camino brillante de Archis) nos entretengan que est├бmos tan agotados
y finalmente nos confiere felicidad
manteni├йndonos, por as├н decirlo, bajo su sombra
que es como la sombra de un sandalia.
